--- PAGE 1 ---
2026 National Leadership Conference  
High School & Middle School Individual Schedules 
Individual Schedules – updated 6/12/2026 
 
Following will be a large ﬁle with preliminary schedules for the 2026 NLC competitive 
events, high school & middle school divisions.  
 
Where can I ﬁnd the o verall Competitive Events Schedule ? 
Visit the NLC page to view the High School and Middle School Schedule of competitive 
events.  
 
I see my event, but what  if I don’t see my name ? 
Some events have multiple sections. Use the search function (Ctrl/Command + f) to 
locate your name. If you still don’t see your name, please contact your Chapter Adviser 
and State Leader for next steps. 
 
When should I show up for the event?  
Objective Test Events  
Arrive at least 15 minutes before the scheduled start time of your objective test. The 
ﬁrst time listed in the conference app is when the test begins. (For example, if your test 
is scheduled from 9:00 AM – 10:00 AM, you will be considered late if you arrive after 
9:00 AM.)  
 
Presentation Events  
The time listed on this schedule is your arrival time. This time includes check-in time. 
Set-up (if allowed) and your presentation will follow in the assigned presentation space. 
 
Where do I show up for the event?  
The location of each event is listed at the top left corner of the schedule.  
 
Can I change my competitive event time?  
Competitive event presentation times cannot be changed or switched to another time. 
To learn more, click here. 
 
Can I observe preliminary presentation events?  
No observers or audience members are allowed for preliminary presentations or 
objective tests. Click here to see which event ﬁnals are available for audience viewing 
and click here for more information about being an audience member. 
 
When will we ﬁnd out presentation ﬁnalists?  
Finalists and their schedules will be posted by 5:00 AM July 1st.
